[38:5] Verily, verily, I say unto you, Whosoever entereth not into the fold of the sheep by the door, but goeth up from another place, that man is a thief and a ,  stealer.

[38:6] But he that entereth by the door is the shepherd of the sheep.

[38:7] And therefore the keeper of the door openeth for him the door; and the sheep hear his voice: and  he calleth his sheep by their names, and they go forth unto him.

[38:8] And when he putteth forth his sheep, he goeth before them, and his sheep follow him: because  they know his voice.

[38:9] And after a stranger will the sheep not go, but they flee from  him: because they hear not the voice of a stranger.

[38:10] This parable spake Jesus unto them: but they knew not what he was saying unto them.

[38:11] Jesus said unto them again, Verily, verily, I say unto you, I am the door of the  sheep.

[38:12] And all that came are thieves and stealers: but the sheep heard them not.

[38:13] I am the door: and if a man enter by me, he shall live, and shall go in and go out,  and shall find pasture.

[38:14] And the stealer cometh not, save that he may steal, and kill, and destroy: but I came that they might have life, and that they might have  the thing that is better.

[38:15] I am the good shepherd; and the good shepherd giveth  himself for his sheep.

[38:16] But the hireling, who is not a shepherd, and whose the sheep are not, when he seeth the wolf as it cometh, leaveth the sheep, and fleeth,  and the wolf cometh, and snatcheth away the sheep, and scattereth them: and the  hireling fleeth because he is an hireling, and hath no care for the sheep.

[38:17] I am the  good shepherd; and I know what is mine, and what is mine knoweth me, as my Father knoweth me, and I know my Father; and I give myself for the sheep.

[38:18] And I have other sheep also, that are not of this flock: them also I must invite, and they shall hear my voice; and all the sheep shall be one, and the shepherd one.

[38:19] Arabic, p.

[38:20] And therefore doth my Father love me, because I give my life, that I may  take it again.

[38:21] No man taketh it from me, but I leave it of my own choice.

[38:22] And I have the right to leave it, and have the right also to take it.

[38:23] And this commandment did I receive of my Father.

[38:24] And there occurred a disagreement among the Jews because of these sayings.

[38:25] And many of them said, He hath a devil, and is afflicted with madness; why listen  ye to him? And others said, These sayings are not those of men possessed with demons.

[38:26] Can a demon haply open the eyes of a blind man?  ,  And the feast of the dedication came on at Jerusalem: and it was winter.

[38:27] And  Jesus was walking in the temple in the porch of Solomon.

[38:28] The Jews therefore surrounded him, and said unto him, Until when dost thou make our hearts anxious?  If thou art the Messiah, tell us plainly.

[38:29] He answered and said unto them, I told you, and ye believe not: and the deeds that I do in my Father's name bear witness ,  to me.

[38:30] But ye believe not, because ye are not of my sheep, as I said unto you.

[38:31] And my sheep hear my voice, and I know them, and they come after me: and I give them eternal life; and they shall not perish for ever, nor shall any man snatch  them out of my hands.

[38:32] For the Father, who hath given them unto me, is greater  than all; and no man is able to take them from the hand of my Father.

[38:33] I and ,  my Father are one.

[38:34] And the Jews took stones to stone him.

[38:35] Jesus said unto them, Many good deeds from my Father have I shewed you; because of which of them,  then, do ye stone me? The Jews said unto him, Not for the good deeds do we stone thee, but because thou blasphemest; and, whilst thou art a man, makest thyself  God.

[38:36] Jesus said unto them, Is it not thus written in your law, I said, Ye are gods?  Arabic, p.

[38:37] And if he called those gods—for to them came the word of God (and it is  not possible in the scripture that anything should be undone)—he then, whom the Father hath sanctified and sent into the world, do ye say that he blasphemeth;  because I said unto you, I am the Son of God? If then I do not the deeds of my  Father, ye believe me not.

[38:38] But if I do, even if ye believe not me, believe the deeds: that ye may know and believe that my Father is in me, and I in my Father.

[38:39] And they sought again to take him: and he went forth out of their hands.

[38:40] And he went beyond Jordan to the place where John was baptizing formerly;  and abode there.

[38:41] And many people came unto him; and they said, John did not  work even one sign: but all that John said of this man is truth.

[38:42] And many believed in him.

[38:43] And there was a sick man, named Lazarus, of the village of Bethany, the brother  of Mary and Martha.

[38:44] And Mary was she that anointed with sweet ointment the feet of Jesus, and wiped them with her hair; and Lazarus, who was sick, was the  brother of this woman.

[38:45] And his sisters sent unto Jesus, and said unto him, Our  Lord, behold, he whom thou lovest is sick.

[38:46] But Jesus said, This sickness is not unto death, but for the glorifying of God, that the Son of God may be glorified ,  because of it.

[38:47] And Jesus loved Martha, and Mary, and Lazarus.

[38:48] And when he  heard that he was sick, he abode in the place where he was two days.

[38:49] And after that,  he said unto his disciples, Come, let us go into Judaea.

[38:50] His disciples said unto him, Our Arabic, p.

[38:51] Master, now the Jews desire to stone thee; and goest thou again thither? ,  Jesus said unto them, Is not the day of twelve hours? If then a man walk in the day, he stumbleth not, because he seeth the light of the world.

[38:52] But if  a man walk in the night, he stumbleth, because there is no lamp in him.

[38:53] This said Jesus: and after that, he said unto them, Lazarus our friend hath fallen asleep; but  I am going to awaken him.

[38:54] His disciples said unto him, Our Lord, if he hath  fallen asleep, he will recover.

[38:55] But Jesus said that concerning his death: while they  supposed that he spake of lying down to sleep.

[38:56] Then Jesus said unto them plainly,  Lazarus is dead.

[38:57] And I am glad that I was not there for your sakes, that ye may  believe; but let us go thither.

[38:58] Thomas, who is called Thama, said to the disciples, his companions, Let us also go, and die with him.

[39:1] Section XXXVIII.

[39:2] ,  And Jesus came to Bethany, and found him already four days in the grave.

[39:3] And Bethany was beside Jerusalem, and its distance from it was a sum of fifteen furlongs;  and many of the Jews came unto Mary and Martha, to comfort their heart  because of their brother.

[39:4] And Martha, when she heard that Jesus had come, went  out to meet him: but Mary was sitting in the house.

[39:5] Martha then said unto Jesus,  My Lord, if thou hadst been here, my brother had not died.

[39:6] But I know now that,  whatever thou shalt ask of God, he will give thee.

[39:7] Jesus said unto her, Thy brother shall  rise.

[39:8] Martha said unto him, I know that he shall rise in the resurrection at the last day.

[39:9] Jesus said unto her, I am the resurrection, and the life: whosoever believeth in  Arabic, p.

[39:10] me, even though he die, he shall live: and every living one that believeth  in me shall never die.

[39:11] Believest thou this? She said unto him, Yea, my Lord: I believe that thou art the Messiah, the Son of God, that cometh into the  world.

[39:12] And when she had said that, she went and called Mary her sister secretly,  and said unto her, Our Master hath come, and summoneth thee.

[39:13] And Mary, when  she heard, rose in haste, and came unto him.

[39:14] (And Jesus then had not come into  the village, but was in the place where Martha met him.

[39:15] ) And the Jews also that were with her in the house, to comfort her, when they saw that Mary rose up and went out in haste, went after her, because they supposed that she was going to the  tomb to weep.

[39:16] And Mary, when she came to where Jesus was, and saw him, fell at his feet, and said unto him, If thou hadst been here, my Lord, my brother had  not died.

[39:17] And Jesus came; and when he saw her weeping, and the Jews that were  with her weeping, he was troubled in himself, and sighed; and he said, In what  place have ye laid him? And they said unto him, Our Lord, come and see.

[39:18] And  the tears of Jesus came.

[39:19] The Jews therefore said, See the greatness of his love for  him! But some of them said, Could not this man, who opened the eyes of that  blind man, have caused that this man also should not die? And Jesus came to the place of burial, being troubled within himself.

[39:20] And the place of burial was a cave,  and a stone was placed at its door.

[39:21] Jesus therefore said, Take these stones away.

[39:22] Martha, the sister of him that was dead, said unto him, My Lord, he hath come to  stink for some time: he hath been four days dead.

[39:23] Jesus said unto her, Did not I say  Arabic, p.

[39:24] unto thee, If thou believest, thou shalt see the glory of God? And they removed those stones.

[39:25] And Jesus lifted his eyes on high, and said, My Father,  I thank thee since thou didst hear me.

[39:26] And I know that thou at all times hearest me: but I say this unto thee because of this multitude that is standing, that they  may believe that thou didst send me.

[39:27] And when he had said that, he cried with a  loud voice, Lazarus, come forth.

[39:28] And that dead man came out, having his hands and feet bound with bandages, and his face wrapped in a scarf.

[39:29] Jesus said unto them, Loose him, and let him go.

[39:30] And many of the Jews which came unto Mary, when they saw the deed of Jesus,  believed in him.

[39:31] But some of them went to the Pharisees, and informed them of all that Jesus did.

[39:32] And the chief priests and the Pharisees gathered, and said, What shall we do?  for lo, this man doeth many signs.

[39:33] And if we leave him thus, all men will believe  in him: and the Romans will come and take our country and people.

[39:34] And one of them, who was called Caiaphas, the chief priest he was in that year, said unto them,  Ye know not anything, nor consider that it is more advantageous for us that one  man should die instead of the people, and not that the whole people perish.

[39:35] And this he said not of himself: but because he was the chief priest of that year, he  prophesied that Jesus was to die instead of the people; and not instead of the people alone, but that he might gather the scattered children of God together.

[39:36] And from that day they considered how to kill him.

[39:37] Arabic, p.

[39:38] And Jesus did not walk openly amongst the Jews, but departed thence to a place near the wilderness, to a town called Ephraim; and he was there, going  about with his disciples.

[39:39] And the passover of the Jews was near: and many went  up from the villages unto Jerusalem before the feast, to purify themselves.

[39:40] And they sought for Jesus, and said one to another in the temple, What think ye of his  holding back from the feast? And the chief priests and the Pharisees had given commandment, that, if any man knew in what place he was, he should reveal it to them, that they might take him.

[39:41] And when the days of his going up were accomplished, he prepared himself that  he might go to Jerusalem.

[39:42] And he sent messengers before him, and departed, and  entered into a village of Samaria, that they might make ready for him.

[39:43] And they  received him not, because he was prepared for going to Jerusalem.

[39:44] And when James and John his disciples saw it, they said unto him, Our Lord, wilt thou that we speak, and fire come down from heaven, to extirpate them, as did Elijah also?  And Jesus turned, and rebuked them, and said, Ye know not of what spirit ye are.

[39:45] Verily the Son of man did not come to destroy lives, but to give life.

[39:46] And they went to another village.

[40:1] Section XXXIX.

[40:2] And Jesus six days before the passover came to Bethany, where was Lazarus,  whom Jesus raised from among the dead.

[40:3] And they made a feast for him there:  and Martha was serving; while Lazarus was one of them that sat with him.

[40:4] And  at the time of Jesus' being at Bethany in the house of Simon the leper, great multitudes of the Jews heard that Jesus was there: and they came, not because of Jesus alone, but Arabic, p.

[40:5] that they might look also on Lazarus, whom he raised from among the dead.

[40:6] ,  And the chief priests considered how they might kill Lazarus also; because  many of the Jews were going on his account, and believing in Jesus.

[40:7] And Mary took a case of the ointment of fine nard, of great price, and opened it, and poured  it out on the head of Jesus as he was reclining; and she anointed his feet, and wiped them with her hair: and the house was filled with the odour of the ointment.

[40:8] ,  But Judas Iscariot, one of the disciples, he that was to betray him, said, Why was  not this ointment sold for three hundred pence, and given unto the poor? This he said, not because of his care for the poor, but because he was a thief, and the chest  was with him, and what was put into it he used to bear.

[40:9] And that displeased the rest of the disciples also within themselves, and they said, Why went this ointment  to waste? It was possible that it should be sold for much, and the poor be given  it.

[40:10] And they were angry with Mary.

[40:11] And Jesus perceived it, and said unto them, Leave her; why molest ye her? a good work hath she accomplished on me: for the  day of my burial kept she it.

[40:12] At all times the poor are with you, and when ye  wish ye can do them a kindness: but I am not at all times with you.

[40:13] And for this cause, when she poured this ointment on my body, it is as if she did it for my burial,  and anointed my body beforehand.

[40:14] And verily I say unto you, In every place where this my gospel shall be proclaimed in all the world, what she did shall be told for a memorial of her.

[40:15] ,  Arabic, p.

[40:16] And when Jesus said that, he went out leisurely to go to Jerusalem.

[40:17] And when he arrived at Bethphage and at Bethany, beside the mount which is  called the mount of Olives, Jesus sent two of his disciples, and he said unto them, Go  into this village that is opposite you: and when ye enter it, ye shall find an ass tied, and  a colt with him, which no man ever yet mounted: loose him, and bring them unto me.

[40:18] And if any man say unto you, Why loose ye them? say unto him thus, We  seek them for our Lord; and straightway send them hither.

[40:19] All this was, that what was said in the prophet might be fulfilled, which said,   Say ye unto the daughter of Zion,  Behold, thy King cometh unto thee,  Meek, and riding upon an ass,  And upon a colt the foal of an ass.

[40:20] And the disciples did not know this at that time: but after that Jesus was glorified, his disciples remembered that these things were written of him, and that this  they had done unto him.

[40:21] And when the two disciples went, they found as he had  said unto them, and they did as Jesus charged them.

[40:22] And when they loosed them,  their owners said unto them, Why loose ye them? They said unto them, We seek  them for our Lord.

[40:23] And they let them go.

[40:24] And they brought the ass and the colt,  and they placed on the colt their garments; and Jesus mounted it.

[40:25] And most of the multitudes spread their garments on the ground before him: and others cut branches  from the trees, and threw them in the way.

[40:26] And when he neared his descent from Arabic, p.

[40:27] the mount of Olives, all the disciples began to rejoice and to praise God with  a loud voice for all the powers which they had seen; and they said, Praise in the highest; Praise to the Son of David: Blessed is he that cometh in the name  of the Lord; and blessed is the kingdom that cometh, that of our father David: Peace in heaven, and praise in the highest.

[40:28] And a great multitude, that which came to the feast, when they heard that Jesus  was coming to Jerusalem, took young palm branches, and went forth to meet him, and cried and said, Praise: Blessed is he that cometh in the name of the Lord, the  King of Israel.

[40:29] Certain therefore of the Pharisees from among the multitudes  said unto him, Our Master, rebuke thy disciples.

[40:30] He said unto them, Verily I say unto you, If these were silent, the stones would cry out.

[40:31] ,  And when he drew near, and saw the city, he wept over it, and said, Would that thou hadst known the things that are for thy peace, in this thy day! now that is  hidden from thine eyes.

[40:32] There shall come unto thee days when thine enemies  shall encompass thee, and straiten thee from every quarter, and shall get possession of thee, and thy children within thee; and they shall not leave in thee a stone upon another; because thou knewest not the time of thy visitation.

[40:33] And when he entered into Jerusalem, the whole city was agitated, and they said,  Who is this? And the multitudes said, This is Jesus, the prophet that is from Nazareth  of Galilee.

[40:34] And the multitude which was with him bare witness that he called  Lazarus from the grave, and raised him from among the dead.

[40:35] And for this cause great multitudes went out to meet him, because they heard the sign which he did.

[41:1] Section XL.

[41:2] Arabic, p.

[41:3] And when Jesus entered the temple, they brought unto him blind and  lame: and he healed them.

[41:4] But when the chief priests and the Pharisees saw the wonders that he did, and the children that were crying in the temple and  saying, Praise be to the Son of David: it distressed them, and they said, Hearest thou not what these say? Jesus said unto them, Yea: did ye not read long ago, From  the mouths of children and infants thou hast chosen my praise? And the Pharisees said one to another, Behold, do ye not see that nothing availeth us? for lo, the whole world hath followed him.

[41:5] And there were among them certain Gentiles also, which had come up to worship  at the feast: these therefore came to Philip, who was of Bethsaida of Galilee,  and asked him, and said unto him, My lord, we wish to see Jesus.

[41:6] And Philip  came and told Andrew: and Andrew and Philip told Jesus.

[41:7] And Jesus answered and said unto them, The hour is come nigh, in which the Son of man is to be glorified.

[41:8] Verily, verily, I say unto you, A grain of wheat, if it fall not and die in the  earth, remaineth alone; but if it die, it beareth much fruit.

[41:9] He that loveth his life destroyeth it; and he that hateth his life in this world shall keep it unto the life eternal.

[41:10] If a man serve me, he will follow me; and where I am, there shall my servant be  also: and whosoever serveth me, the Father will honour him.

[41:11] Now is my soul troubled: Arabic, p.

[41:12] and what shall I say? My Father, deliver me from this hour.

[41:13] But  for this cause came I unto this hour.

[41:14] My Father, glorify thy name.

[41:15] And a  voice was heard from heaven, I have glorified it, and shall glorify it.

[41:16] And the multitude that were standing heard, and said, This is thunder: and others said, An  angel speaketh to him.

[41:17] Jesus answered and said unto them, Not because of me  was this voice, but because of you.

[41:18] Now is the judgement of this world; and the  prince of this world shall now be cast forth.

[41:19] And I, when I am lifted up from the  earth, shall draw every man unto me.

[41:20] This he said, that he might shew by what  manner of death he should die.

[41:21] The multitudes said unto him, We have heard out of the law that the Messiah abideth for ever: how then sayest thou, that the Son of  man is to be lifted up? who is this, the Son of man? Jesus said unto them, Another little while is the light with you.

[41:22] Walk so long as ye have light, lest the darkness overtake you; for he that walketh in the darkness knoweth not whither he goeth.

[41:23] So long as ye have light, believe the light, that ye may be the children of the light.

[41:24] And when certain of the Pharisees asked of Jesus, when the kingdom of God should come, he answered and said unto them, The kingdom of God cometh not  with expectation: neither shall they say, Lo, it is here! nor, Lo, it is there! for the kingdom of God is within you.

[41:25] And in the daytime he was teaching in the temple; and at night he used to go  out, and pass the night in the mount called the mount of Olives.

[41:26] And all the people came to him in the morning in the temple, to hear his word.

[41:27] ,  Then spake Jesus unto the multitudes and his disciples, and said unto them, On  Arabic, p.

[41:28] the seat of Moses are seated the scribes and Pharisees: everything that they say unto you now to keep, keep and do: but according to their deeds  do ye not; for they say, and do not.

[41:29] And they bind heavy burdens, and lay them on the shoulders of the people; while they with one of their fingers will not come ,  near them.

[41:30] But all their deeds they do to make a shew before men.

[41:31] And all the multitude were hearing that with pleasure.

[41:32] And in the course of his teaching he said unto them, Guard yourselves from the  scribes, who desire to walk in robes, and love salutation in the marketplaces, and sitting in the highest places of the synagogues, and at feasts in the highest parts of  the rooms: and they broaden their amulets, and lengthen the cords of their cloaks,  and love that they should be called by men, My master, and devour widows' houses, because of their prolonging their prayers; these then shall receive greater judgement.

[41:33] But ye, be ye not called masters: for your master is one; all ye are brethren.

[41:34] Call not then to yourselves any one father on earth: for your Father is one, who is  in heaven.

[41:35] And be not called directors: for your director is one, even the Messiah.

[41:36] ,  He that is great among you shall be unto you a minister.

[41:37] Whosoever shall exalt himself shall be abased; and whosoever shall abase himself shall be exalted.

[41:38] Woe unto you, Pharisees! because ye love the highest places in the synagogues, and salutation in the marketplaces.

[41:39] Woe unto you, scribes and Pharisees, hypocrites! because ye devour widows' houses, because of your prolonging your prayers: for this reason then ye shall receive greater judgement.

[41:40] Woe unto you, scribes and Pharisees, hypocrites! because ye have shut the kingdom of God before men.

[41:41] Arabic, p.

[41:42] Woe unto you that know the law! for ye concealed the keys of knowledge: ye enter not, and those that are entering ye suffer not to enter.

[41:43] Woe unto you, scribes and Pharisees, hypocrites! because ye compass land and sea to draw one proselyte; and when he is become so, ye make him a son of hell twice as much as yourselves.

[41:44] Woe unto you, ye blind guides! because ye say, Whosoever sweareth by the temple, it is nothing; but whosoever sweareth by the gold that is in the temple,  shall be condemned.

[41:45] Ye blind foolish ones: which is greater, the gold, or the  temple which sanctifieth the gold? And, Whosoever sweareth by the altar, it is nothing; but whosoever sweareth by the offering that is upon it, shall be condemned.

[41:46] Ye blind foolish ones: which is greater, the offering, or the altar which sanctifieth  the offering? Whosoever then sweareth by the altar, hath sworn by it, and by all  that is upon it.

[41:47] And whosoever sweareth by the temple, hath sworn by it, and by  him that is dwelling in it.

[41:48] And whosoever sweareth by heaven, hath sworn by the throne of God, and by him that sitteth upon it.

[41:49] Woe unto you, scribes and Pharisees, hypocrites! because ye tithe mint and rue and dill and cummin and all herbs, and ye leave the important matters of the law, judgement, and mercy, and faith, and the love of God: this ought ye to do, and  not to leave that undone.

[41:50] Ye blind guides, which strain out a gnat, and swallow camels.

[41:51] Woe unto you, scribes and Pharisees, hypocrites! because ye cleanse the outside of the cup and of the platter, while the inside of them is full of injustice and wrong.

[41:52] Ye blind Pharisees, cleanse first the inside of the cup and of the platter, then shall the outside of them be cleansed.

[41:53] Arabic, p.

[41:54] Woe unto you, scribes and Pharisees, hypocrites! because ye resemble whited sepulchres, which appear from the outside beautiful, but within  full of the bones of the dead, and all uncleanness.

[41:55] So ye also from without appear unto men like the righteous, but within ye are full of wrong and hypocrisy.

[41:56] One of the scribes answered and said unto him, Teacher, in this saying of thine  thou art casting a slur on us.

[41:57] He said, And to you also, ye scribes, woe! for ye lade men with heavy burdens, and ye with one of your fingers come not near those burdens.

[41:58] Woe unto you, scribes and Pharisees, hypocrites! for ye build the tombs of the prophets, which your fathers killed, and adorn the burying-places of the righteous,  and say, If we had been in the days of our fathers, we should not have been partakers  with them in the blood of the prophets.

[41:59] Wherefore, behold, ye witness against  yourselves, that ye are the children of those that slew the prophets.

[41:60] And ye also,  ye fill up the measure of your fathers.

[41:61] Ye serpents, ye children of vipers, where shall ye flee from the judgement of Gehenna?.

[42:1] Section XLI.

[42:2] Therefore, behold, I, the wisdom of God, am sending unto you prophets, and apostles, and wise men, and scribes: and some of them ye shall slay and crucify; and some of them ye shall beat in your synagogues, and persecute from city to  city: that there may come on you all the blood of the righteous that hath been poured upon the ground from the blood of Abel the pure to the blood of Zachariah the son of Barachiah, whom ye slew between the temple and the altar.

[42:3] Verily I say unto you, All these things shall come upon this generation.

[42:4] Arabic, p.

[42:5] O Jerusalem, Jerusalem, slayer of the prophets, and stoner of them that are sent unto her! how many times did I wish to gather thy children, as  a hen gathereth her chickens under her wings, and ye would not! Your house shall  be left over you desolate.

[42:6] Verily I say unto you, Ye shall not see me henceforth, till ye shall say Blessed is he that cometh in the name of the Lord.

[42:7] And many of the rulers also believed on him; but because of the Pharisees they  were not confessing him, lest they be put out of the synagogue: and they loved  the praise of men more than the praising of God.

[42:8] And Jesus cried and said,  Whosoever believeth in me, believeth not in me, but in him that sent me.

[42:9] And  whosoever seeth me hath seen him that sent me.

[42:10] I am come a light into the  world, and so every one that believeth in me abideth not in the darkness.

[42:11] And whosoever heareth my sayings, and keepeth them not, I judge him not: for I came  not to judge the world, but to give the world life.

[42:12] Whosoever wrongeth me, and receiveth not my sayings, there is one that judgeth him: the word that I spake, it  shall judge him at the last day.

[42:13] I from myself did not speak: but the Father which sent me, he hath given me commandment, what I should say, and what I  should speak; and I know that his commandment is eternal life.

[42:14] The things that I say now, as my Father hath said unto me, even so I say.

[42:15] And when he said that unto them, the scribes and Pharisees began their evil-doing, being angry with him, and finding fault with his sayings, and harassing him  in many things; seeking to catch something from his mouth, that they might be able to calumniate him.

[42:16] And when there gathered together myriads of great multitudes, which almost trode Arabic, p.

[42:17] one upon another, Jesus began to say unto his disciples, Preserve yourselves  from the leaven of the Pharisees, which is hypocrisy.

[42:18] For there is nothing  concealed, that shall not be revealed: nor hid, that shall not be known.

[42:19] Everything that ye have said in the darkness shall be heard in the light; and what ye have spoken secretly in the ears in the inner chambers shall be proclaimed on the roofs.

[42:20] ,  This said Jesus, and he went and hid himself from them.

[42:21] But notwithstanding  his having done all these signs before them, they believed not in him: that the word of Isaiah the prophet might be fulfilled, who said,  My Lord, who is he that hath believed to hear us?  And the arm of the Lord, to whom hath it appeared?   And for this reason it is not possible for them to believe, because Isaiah also said,   They have blinded their eyes, and made dark their heart;  That they may not see with their eyes, and understand with their heart,  And turn,  So that I should heal them.

[42:22] This said Isaiah when he saw his glory, and spake of him.

[42:23] And when Jesus went out of the temple, certain of his disciples came forward  to shew him the buildings of the temple, and its beauty and greatness, and the strength of the stones that were laid in it, and the elegance of its building, and that  it was adorned with noble stones and beautiful colours.

[42:24] Jesus answered and said  unto them, See ye these great buildings? verily I say unto you, Days will come, when there shall not be left here a stone upon another, that shall not be cast down.

[42:25] And two days before the passover of unleavened bread, the chief priests and  the scribes sought how they might take him by deceit, and kill him: and they said, It shall not be at the feast, lest the people be agitated.

[42:26] And when Jesus sat on the mount of Olives opposite the temple, his disciples, Simon Cephas and James and John and Andrew, came forward unto him, and said unto him  between themselves and him, Teacher, tell us when that shall be, and what is the sign  Arabic, p.

[42:27] of thy coming and the end of the world.

[42:28] Jesus answered and said unto them, Days will come, when ye shall long to see one of the days of the Son of ,  man, and shall not behold.

[42:29] Take heed lest any man lead you astray.

[42:30] Many shall  come in my name, and say, I am the Messiah; and they shall say, The time is come  near, and shall lead many astray: go not therefore after them.

[42:31] And when ye hear of wars and tidings of insurrections, see to it, be not agitated: for these things must  first be; only the end is not yet come.

[42:32] Nation shall rise against nation, and kingdom  against kingdom: and great earthquakes shall be in one place and another, and there shall be famines and deaths and agitations: and there shall be fear and terror and great signs that shall appear from heaven, and there shall be great ,  storms All these things are the beginning of travail.

[42:33] But before all of that, they shall lay hands upon you, and persecute you, and deliver you unto the synagogues  and into prisons, and bring you before kings and judges for my name's sake.

[42:34] And  that shall be unto you for a witness.

[42:35] But first must my gospel be preached unto all  nations.

[42:36] And when they bring you into the synagogues before the rulers and the authorities, be not anxious beforehand how ye shall answer for yourselves, or what ye ,  shall say: because it is not ye that speak, but the Holy Spirit.

[42:37] Lay it to your heart, not  Arabic, p.

[42:38] to be anxious before the time what ye shall say: and I shall give you understanding and wisdom, which all your adversaries shall not be able to gainsay.

[42:39] And then shall they deliver you unto constraint, and shall kill you: and ye shall be  hated of all nations because of my name.

[42:40] And then shall many go astray, and they  shall hate one another, and deliver one another unto death.

[42:41] And your parents, and your brethren, and your kinsfolk, and your friends shall deliver you up, and shall ,  slay some of you.

[42:42] But a lock of hair from your heads shall not perish.

[42:43] And by  your patience ye shall gain your souls.

[42:44] And many men, false prophets, shall arise,  and lead many astray.

[42:45] And because of the abounding of iniquity, the love of many  shall wax cold.

[42:46] But he that endureth to the end, the same shall be saved.

[42:47] And  this, the gospel of the kingdom, shall be preached in all the world for a testimony to all nations; and then shall come the end of all.

[43:1] Section XLII.

[43:2] But when ye see Jerusalem with the army compassing it about, then know that  its desolation is come near.

[43:3] Those then that are in Judaea at that time shall flee to the mountain; and those that are within her shall flee; and those that are in the  villages shall not enter her.

[43:4] For these days are the days of vengeance, that all that  is written may be fulfilled.

[43:5] And when ye see the unclean sign of desolation, spoken of in Daniel the prophet, standing in the pure place, he that readeth shall understand, ,  and then he that is in Judaea shall flee in to the mountain: and let him that is on the  roof not go down, nor enter in to take anything from his house: and let him that is in  Arabic, p.

[43:6] the field not turn behind him to take his garment.

[43:7] Woe to them that are with child and to them that give suck in those days! there shall be great  distress in the land, and wrath against this nation.

[43:8] And they shall fall on the edge of the sword, and shall be taken captive to every land: and Jerusalem shall be trodden down of the nations, until the times of the nations be ended.

[43:9] Then if any man say unto you, The Messiah is here; or, Lo, he is there; believe  him not: there shall rise then false Messiahs and prophets of lying, and shall do signs and wonders, in order that they may lead astray even the elect also, if they  be able.

[43:10] But as for you, beware: for I have acquainted you with everything  beforehand.

[43:11] If then they say unto you, Lo, he is in the desert; go not out, lest ye  be taken: and if they say unto you, Lo, he is in the chamber; believe not.

[43:12] And as the lightning appeareth from the east, and is seen unto the west; so shall be the  coming of the Son of man.

[43:13] But first he must suffer much and be rejected by this  generation.

[43:14] Pray therefore that your flight be not in winter, nor on a sabbath:  there shall be then great tribulation, the like of which there hath not been from the  beginning of the world till now, nor shall be.

[43:15] And except the Lord had shortened those days, no flesh would have lived: but because of the elect, whom he elected,  he shortened those days.

[43:16] And there shall be signs in the sun and the moon and the stars; and upon the earth affliction of the nations, and rubbing of hands for the confusion  Arabic, p.

[43:17] of the noise of the sea, and an earthquake: the souls of men shall  go forth from fear of that which is to come upon the earth.

[43:18] And in those days, straightway after the distress of those days, the sun shall become dark, and the moon shall not shew its light, and the stars shall fall from heaven, and the powers  of heaven shall be convulsed: and then shall appear the sign of the Son of man in heaven: and at that time all the tribes of the earth shall wail, and look unto the Son  of man coming on the clouds of heaven with power and much glory.

[43:19] And he shall send his angels with the great trumpet, and they shall gather his elect from the four  winds, from one end of heaven to the other.

[43:20] But when these things begin to be, be of good cheer, and lift up your heads; for your salvation is come near.

[43:21] Learn the example of the fig tree: when it letteth down its branches, and putteth  forth its leaves, ye know that the summer is come; so ye also, when ye see these things begun to be, know ye that the kingdom of God hath arrived at the  door.

[43:22] Verily I say unto you, This generation shall not pass away, until all these  things shall be.

[43:23] Heaven and earth shall pass away, but my sayings shall not pass away.

[43:24] Take heed to yourselves, that your hearts become not heavy with inordinate desire, and drunkenness, and the care of the world at any time, and that day come  upon you suddenly: for it is as a shock that shocks all the inhabitants that are on the  face of the whole earth.

[43:25] Watch at all times, and pray, that ye may be worthy to escape Arabic, p.

[43:26] from all the things that are to be, and that ye may stand before the Son of  man.

[43:27] Of that day and of that hour hath no man learned, not even the angels  of heaven, neither the Son, but the Father.

[43:28] See ye, and watch and pray: for ye know  not when that time will be.

[43:29] It is as a man, who journeyed, and left his house, and gave his authority to his servants, and appointed every man to his work, and  charged the porter to be wakeful.

[43:30] Be wakeful then: since ye know not when the lord of the house cometh, in the evening, or in the middle of the night, or when the  cock croweth, or in the morning; lest he come unexpectedly, and find you sleeping.

[43:31] The thing that I say unto you, unto all of you do I say it, Be ye watchful.

[43:32] For as it was in the days of Noah, so shall the coming of the Son of man be.

[43:33] As they were before the flood eating and drinking, and taking wives, and giving  wives to men, until the day in which Noah entered into the ark, and they perceived not till the flood came, and took them all; so shall the coming of the Son of man  be.

[43:34] And as it was in the days of Lot; they were eating and drinking, and selling  and buying, and planting and building, on the day in which Lot went out from Sodom, and the Lord rained fire and brimstone from heaven, and destroyed them ,  all: so shall it be in the day in which the Son of man is revealed.

[43:35] And in that day, whosoever is on the roof, and his garments in the house, let him not go down to  take them: and he that is in the field shall not turn behind him.

[43:36] Remember Lot's  wife.

[43:37] Whosoever shall desire to save his life shall destroy it: but whosoever shall  destroy his life shall save it.

[43:38] Verily I say unto you, In that night there shall be two on  Arabic, p.

[43:39] one bed; one shall be taken, and another left.

[43:40] And two women shall be grinding  at one mill; one shall be taken, and another left.

[43:41] And two shall be in the  field; one shall be taken, and another left.

[43:42] They answered and said unto him, To what place, our Lord? He said unto them, Where the body is, there will the eagles ,  gather.

[43:43] Be attentive now: for ye know not at what hour your Lord cometh.

[43:44] Know this: if the master of the house had known in what watch the thief would come, he would have been attentive, and would not make it possible that his house should be  broken through.

[43:45] Therefore be ye also ready: for in the hour that ye think not the Son of man cometh.

[44:1] Section XLIII.

[44:2] Simon Cephas said unto him, Our Lord, is it to us that thou hast spoken this  parable, or also to every man? Jesus said unto him, Who, thinkest thou, is the servant, the master of the house, trusted with control, whom his lord set over his  household, to give them their food in its season? Blessed is that servant, whom his  lord shall come and find having done so.

[44:3] Verily I say unto you, He will set him  over all that he hath.

[44:4] But if that evil servant say in his heart, My lord delayeth his  coming; and shall begin to beat his servants and the maidservants of his lord, and  shall begin to eat and to drink with the drunken; the lord of that servant shall come  in the day that he thinketh not, and in the hour that he knoweth not, and shall Arabic, p.

[44:5] judge him, and appoint his portion with the hypocrites, and with those that are not faithful: there shall be weeping and gnashing of teeth.

[44:6] Then shall the kingdom of heaven be like unto ten virgins, those that took their  lamps, and went forth to meet the bridegroom and the bride.

[44:7] Five of them were  wise, and five foolish.

[44:8] And those foolish ones took their lamps, and took not with ,  them oil: but those wise ones took oil in vessels along with their lamps.

[44:9] When then  the bridegroom delayed, they all slumbered and slept.

[44:10] But in the middle of the night there occurred a cry, Behold, the bridegroom cometh! Go forth therefore to ,  meet him.

[44:11] Then all those virgins arose, and made ready their lamps.

[44:12] The foolish  said unto the wise, Give us of your oil; for our lamps are gone out.

[44:13] But those wise answered and said, Perhaps there will not be enough for us and you: but go ye to  the sellers, and buy for yourselves.

[44:14] And when they went away to buy, the bridegroom came; and those that were ready went in with him to the marriage feast: and  the door was shut.

[44:15] And at last those other virgins also came and said, Our Lord,  our Lord, open unto us.

[44:16] He answered and said unto them, Verily I say unto you,  I know you not.

[44:17] Watch then, for ye know not that day nor that hour.

[44:18] It is as a man, who went on a journey, and called his servants, and delivered unto  them his possessions.

[44:19] And unto one he gave five talents, and another two, and another  one; every one according to his strength; and went on his journey forthwith.

[44:20] He Arabic, p.

[44:21] then that received the five talents went and traded with them, and gained  other five.

[44:22] And so also he of the two gained other two.

[44:23] But he that received  the one went and digged in the earth, and hid the money of his lord.

[44:24] And after a long time the lord of those servants came, and took from them the account.

[44:25] And he that received five talents came near and brought other five, and said, My lord, thou gavest me five talents: lo, I have gained other five in addition to them.

[44:26] His lord said unto him, Well done, thou good and faithful servant: over a little hast  thou been faithful, over much will I set thee: enter into the joy of thy lord.

[44:27] And he that had the two came near and said, My lord, thou gavest me two talents: lo,  other two have I gained in addition to them.

[44:28] His lord said unto him, Good, thou faithful servant: over a little hast thou been faithful, over much will I set thee: enter  into the joy of thy lord.

[44:29] And he also that received the one talent came forward and said, My lord, I knew thee that thou art a severe man, who reapest where thou  sowest not, and gatherest where thou didst not scatter: and so I was afraid, and  went away and hid thy talent in the earth: lo, thou hast what is thine.

[44:30] His lord answered and said unto him, Thou wicked and slothful servant, thou knewest me  that I reap where I sowed not, and gather where I did not scatter; it was incumbent on thee to put my money to the bank, and then I should come and seek it with its  gains.

[44:31] Take now from him the talent, and give it to him that hath ten talents.

[44:32] Whosoever hath shall be given, and he shall have more: but he that hath not, even  Arabic, p.

[44:33] what he hath shall be taken from him.

[44:34] And the unprofitable servant, put him forth into the outer darkness: there shall be the weeping and gnashing of teeth.

[44:35] ,  Your loins shall be girded, and your lamps lit; and ye shall be like the people that are looking for their lord, when he shall return from the feast; so that, when  he cometh and knocketh, they may at once open unto him.

[44:36] Blessed are those servants, whom their lord shall come and find attentive: verily I say unto you, that he will gird his waist, and make them sit down, and pass through them and serve  them.

[44:37] And if he come in the second watch, or the third, and find thus, blessed are those servants.

[44:38] But when the Son of man cometh in his glory, and all his pure angels with him,  then shall he sit on the throne of his glory: and he will gather before him all the nations, and separate them the one from the other, like the shepherd who separateth  the sheep from the goats; and will set the sheep on his right, and the goats on his  left.

[44:39] Then shall the King say to those that are at his right, Come, ye blessed of my Father, inherit the kingdom prepared for you from the foundations of the world:  I hungered, and ye gave me to eat; and I thirsted, and ye gave me to drink; and I  was a stranger, and ye took me in; and I was naked, and ye clothed me; and I  was sick, and ye visited me; and I was in prison, and ye cared for me.

[44:40] Then shall those righteous say unto him, Our Lord, when saw we thee hungry, and fed thee?  or thirsty, and gave thee to drink? And when saw we thee a stranger, and took  thee in? or naked, and clothed thee? And when saw we thee sick, or imprisoned, and  cared for thee? The King shall answer and say unto them, Verily I say unto you, What  Arabic, p.

[44:41] ye did to one of these my brethren, the little ones, ye did unto me.

[44:42] Then shall he say unto those that are on his left also, Depart from me, ye cursed,  into the eternal fire prepared for the devil and his hosts: I hungered, and ye fed me  not; and I thirsted, and ye did not give me to drink; and I was a stranger, and ye took me not in; and I was naked, and ye clothed me not; and I was sick, and imprisoned,  and ye visited me not.

[44:43] Then shall those also answer and say, Our Lord, when saw we thee an hungred, or athirst, or naked, or a stranger, or sick, or imprisoned,  and did not minister unto thee? Then shall he answer and say unto them, Verily I say unto you, When ye did it not unto one of these little ones, ye did it not  unto me also.

[44:44] And these shall go away into eternal punishment: but the righteous into eternal life.

[45:1] Section XLIV.

[45:2] ,  And when Jesus finished all these sayings, he said unto his disciples, Ye know that after two days will be the passover, and the Son of man is delivered up to be  crucified.

[45:3] Then gathered together the chief priests, and the scribes, and the elders  of the people, unto the court of the chief priest, who was called Caiaphas; and they took counsel together concerning Jesus, that they might seize him by subtilty, and  kill him.

[45:4] But they said, Not during the feast, lest there take place a disturbance among the people; for they feared the people.

[45:5] And Satan entered into Judas who was called Iscariot, who was of the number  of the twelve.

[45:6] And he went away, and communed with the chief priests, and the scribes, and those that held command in the temple, and said unto them, What  Arabic, p.

[45:7] would ye pay me, and I will deliver him unto you? And they, when they heard it, were pleased, and made ready for him thirty pieces of money.

[45:8] And he promised them, and from that time he sought an opportunity that he might deliver unto them Jesus without the multitude.

[45:9] And on the first day of unleavened bread the disciples came to Jesus, and said unto him, Where wilt thou that we go and make ready for thee that thou mayest eat the passover?   And before the feast of the passover, Jesus knew that the hour was arrived for his departure from this world unto his Father; and he loved his own in this world,  and to the last he loved them.

[45:10] And at the time of the feast, Satan put into the  heart of Judas, the son of Simon Iscariot, to deliver him up.

[45:11] And Jesus, because he knew that the Father had delivered into his hands everything, and that he came  forth from the Father, and goeth unto God, rose from supper, and laid aside his  garments; and took a towel, and girded his waist, and poured water into a bason, and began to wash the feet of his disciples, and to wipe them with the towel wherewith  his waist was girded.

[45:12] And when he came to Simon Cephas, Simon said unto  him, Dost thou, my Lord, wash for me my feet? Jesus answered and said unto  him, What I do, now thou knowest not; but afterwards thou shalt learn.

[45:13] Simon said unto him, Thou shalt never wash for me my feet.

[45:14] Jesus said unto him, If I  wash thee not, thou hast no part with me.

[45:15] Simon Cephas said unto him, Then, my  Lord, wash not for me my feet alone, but my hands also and my head.

[45:16] Jesus said unto him, He that batheth needeth not to wash save his feet, whereas his whole  body is clean: and ye also are clean, but not all of you.

[45:17] For Jesus knew him that should betray him; therefore said he, Ye are not all clean.

[45:18] Arabic, p.

[45:19] So when he had washed their feet, he took his garments, and sat down, and  said unto them, Know ye what I have done unto you? Ye call me, Master,  and, Lord: and ye say well; so I am.

[45:20] If then I, now, who am your Lord and Master, have washed for you your feet, how needful is it that ye should wash one another's feet!  This have I given you as an example, that as I have done to you so ye should do  also.

[45:21] Verily, verily, I say unto you, No servant is greater than his lord; nor an  apostle greater than he that sent him.

[45:22] If ye know that, ye are happy if ye do it.

[45:23] My saying this is not for all of you: for I know whom I have chosen: but that the scripture might be fulfilled, He that eateth with me bread lifted against me his  heel.

[45:24] Henceforth I say unto you before it come to pass, that, when it cometh to  pass, ye may believe that I am he.

[45:25] Verily, verily, I say unto you, Whosoever receiveth whomsoever I send receiveth me; and whosoever receiveth me receiveth him that sent me.

[45:26] Who is the great one, he that sitteth, or he that serveth? is it not he that sitteth?  I am among you as he that serveth.

[45:27] But ye are they that have continued with me  in my temptations; I promise you, as my Father promised me, the kingdom, that ye may eat and drink at the table of my kingdom.

[45:28] And the first day came, the feast of unleavened bread, on which the Jews were  wont to sacrifice the passover.

[45:29] And Jesus sent two of his disciples, Cephas and John, and said unto them, Go and make ready for us the passover, that we may eat.

[45:30] ,  And they said unto him, Where wilt thou that we make ready for thee? He said unto them, Go, enter the city; and at the time of your entering, there shall meet you a man bearing a pitcher of water; follow him, and the place where he entereth, say  to such an one, the master of the house, Our Master saith, My time is come, and Arabic, p.

[45:31] at thy house I keep the passover.

[45:32] Where then is the lodging-place where  I shall eat with my disciples? And he will shew you a large upper room  spread and made ready: there then make ready for us.

[45:33] And his two disciples went out, and came to the city, and found as he had said unto them: and they made ready the passover as he had said unto them.

[45:34] And when the evening was come, and the time arrived, Jesus came and reclined,  and the twelve apostles with him.

[45:35] And he said unto them, With desire I have  desired to eat this passover with you before I suffer: I say unto you, that henceforth I shall not eat it, until it is fulfilled in the kingdom of God.

[45:36] Jesus said that, and was agitated in his spirit, and testified, and said, Verily,  verily, I say unto you, One of you, he that eateth with me, shall betray me.

[45:37] And they were very sorrowful; and they began to say unto him, one after another of  them, Can it be I, Lord? He answered and said unto them, One of the twelve,  he that dippeth his hand with me in the dish, will betray me.

[45:38] And lo, the hand of  him that betrayeth me is on the table.

[45:39] And the Son of man goeth, as it is written of him: woe then to that man by whose hand the Son of man is betrayed! for it  would have been better for that man had he not been born.

[45:40] And the disciples  looked one on another, for they knew not to whom he referred; and they began to search among themselves, who that might be who was to do this.

[46:1] Section XLV.

[46:2] ,  Arabic, p.

[46:3] And one of his disciples was sitting in his bosom, he whom Jesus loved.

[46:6] And Jesus dipped bread, and gave to Judas, the son of Simon Iscariot.

[46:7] And after the bread, Satan entered him.

[46:9] And no man of them that sat knew why he  said this unto him.

[46:10] And some of them thought, because Judas had the box, that he was bidding him buy what would be needed for the feast; or, that he might pay  something to the poor.

[46:25] By this shall every man know that ye are  my disciples, if ye have love one to another.

[46:32] Arabic, p.

[46:34] But Cephas said the more, Even if it lead to death with thee, I shall not deny thee, my Lord.

[46:35] And in like manner said all the disciples also.

[46:39] And if I go to prepare for you a place, I shall return again, and take you unto me: and so where I am, there ye ,  shall be also.

[46:40] And the place that I go ye know, and the way ye know.

[46:42] And if ye had known me, ye should have known my Father: and from henceforth ye know him,  and have seen him.

[46:43] Philip said unto him, Our Lord, shew us the Father, and it sufficeth  us.
