Believest thou not that I am in my Father, and my Father in me? and the saying that I say, I say not of myself: but my Father who dwelleth in  me, he doeth these deeds.

[46:45] Believe that I am in my Father, and my Father in me:  Arabic, p.

[46:46] or else believe for the sake of the deeds.

[46:47] Verily, verily, I say unto you, Whosoever believeth in me, the deeds that I do shall he do also; and  more than that shall he do: I go unto the Father.

[46:48] And what ye shall ask in my  name, I shall do unto you, that the Father may be glorified in his Son.

[46:49] And if ye ,  ask me in my name, I will do it.

[46:50] If ye love me, keep my commandments.

[46:51] And I will entreat of my Father, and he will send unto you another Paraclete, that he  may be with you for ever, even the Spirit of truth: whom the world cannot receive; for it hath not seen him, nor known him: but ye know him; for he hath dwelt  with you, and is in you.

[46:52] I will not leave you orphans: I will come unto you.

[46:53] Another little while, and the world seeth me not; but ye see me that I live, and ye  shall live also.

[46:54] And in that day ye shall know that I am in my Father, and ye in me, and I in you.

[47:1] Section XLVI.

[47:2] Whosoever hath my commandments, and keepeth them, he it is that loveth me: and he that loveth me shall be loved of my Father, and I will love him, and will  shew myself unto him.

[47:3] Judas (not Iscariot) said unto him, My Lord, what is the  purpose of thy intention to shew thyself to us, and not to the world? Jesus answered and said unto him, Whosoever loveth me will keep my word: and my Father will love him, and to him will we come, and make our abode with him.

[47:4] But he that loveth me not keepeth not my word: and this word that ye hear is not my word, but the Father's which sent me.

[47:5] ,  This have I spoken unto you, while I was yet with you.

[47:6] But the Paraclete, the Holy Spirit, whom my Father will send in my name, he will teach you everything, and  Arabic, p.

[47:7] he will bring to your remembrance all that I say unto you.

[47:8] Peace I leave you; my peace I give unto you: and not as this world giveth, give I unto you.

[47:9] Let your heart not be troubled, nor fearful.

[47:10] Ye heard that I said unto you, that I go away, and come unto you.

[47:11] If ye loved me, ye would rejoice, that I go away to my  Father: for my Father is greater than I.

[47:12] And now I say unto you before it come  to pass, that, when it cometh to pass, ye may believe me.

[47:13] Now I will not speak with you much: the Archon of the world will come, and he will have nothing in  me: but that the world may know that I love my Father, and as my Father charged me, so I do.

[47:14] And he said unto them, When I sent you without purses, or wallets, and shoes,  lacked ye perchance anything? They said unto him, Nothing.

[47:15] He said unto them, Henceforth, whosoever hath a purse, let him take it, and likewise the wallet also: and whosoever hath not a sword, shall sell his garment, and buy for himself a  sword.

[47:16] I say unto you, that this scripture also must be fulfilled in me, that I should be reckoned with the transgressors: for all that is said of me is fulfilled in  me.

[47:17] His disciples said unto him, Our Lord, lo, here are two swords.

[47:18] He said  unto them, They are sufficient.

[47:19] Arise, let us go hence.

[47:20] And they arose, and praised, and went forth, and went, according to their custom, to the mount of Olives, he and his disciples.

[47:21] And he said unto them, I am the true vine, and my Father is the husbandman.

[47:22] Every branch that produceth not fruit in me, he taketh it: and that which giveth fruit,  he cleanseth it, that it may give much fruit.

[47:23] Ye are already clean because of the word  that I have spoken unto you.

[47:24] Abide in me, and I in you.

[47:25] And as the branch of the Arabic, p.

[47:26] vine cannot produce fruit of itself, if it be not abiding in the vine; so too ye  also, if ye abide not in me.

[47:27] I am the vine, and ye are the branches: He then that abideth in me, and I in him, he giveth much fruit: for without me ye cannot  do anything.

[47:28] And if a man abide not in me, he is cast without, like a withered  branch; and it is gathered, and cast into the fire, that it may be burned.

[47:29] If ye abide in me, and my word abide in you, everything that ye desire to ask shall be  done unto you.

[47:30] And herein is the Father glorified, that ye may give much fruit;  and ye shall be my disciples.

[47:31] And as my Father loved me, I loved you also:  abide in my love.

[47:32] If ye keep my commands, ye shall abide in my love; as I have  kept my Father's commands, and abode in his love.

[47:33] I have spoken that unto you,  that my joy may be in you, and your joy be fulfilled.

[47:34] This is my commandment,  that ye love one another, as I loved you.

[47:35] And no love is greater than this, namely,  that a man should give his life for his friends.

[47:36] Ye are my friends, if ye do all that  I command you.

[47:37] I call you not now servants; for the servant knoweth not what his lord doeth: my friends have I now called you; for everything that I heard from  my Father I have made known unto you.

[47:38] Ye did not choose me, but I chose I you, and appointed you, that ye also should go and bear fruit, and that your fruit should  abide; and that all that ye shall ask my Father in my name, he may give you.

[47:39] This  I command you, that ye love one another.

[47:40] And if the world hate you, know that  before you it hated me.

[47:41] If then ye were of the world, the world would love its own: but ye are not of the world: I chose you out of the world: therefore the world  Arabic, p.

[47:42] hateth you.

[47:43] Remember the word that I said unto you, that no servant is greater than his lord.

[47:44] And if they persecuted me, you also will they  persecute; and if they kept my word, your word also will they keep.

[47:45] But all these things will they do unto you for my name's sake, for they have not known him  that sent me.

[47:46] And if I had not come and spoken unto them, they had not had sin:  but now they have no excuse for their sins.

[47:47] Whosoever hateth me, also hateth my  Father.

[47:48] And if I had not done the deeds before them that no other man did, they would not have had sin: but now they have seen and hated me and my Father  also: that the word may be fulfilled that is written in their law, They hated me for  nothing.

[47:49] But when the Paraclete is come, whom I will send unto you from my Father, even the Spirit of truth, which goeth forth from my Father, he shall bear witness of  me: and ye also bear witness, because from the beginning ye have been with me.

[47:50] ,  I have said that unto you, that ye may not stumble.

[47:51] And they shall put you out of their synagogues: and there cometh an hour when every one that killeth  you shall think that he hath offered unto God an offering.

[47:52] And they will do that,  because they do not know me, nor my Father.

[47:53] I have said that unto you, so that  when its time is come, ye may remember it, that I told you.

[47:54] And this hitherto I said not unto you, because I was with you.

[47:55] But now I go unto him that sent me; and no  man of you asketh me whither I go.

[47:56] I have said that unto you now, and grief hath  come and taken possession of your hearts But I say the truth unto you; It is better for you that I go away: for if I go not away, the Paraclete will not come unto you;  Arabic, p.

[47:57] but if I go away, I will send him unto you.

[47:58] And when he cometh, he will reprove the world for sin, and for righteousness, and for judgement: ,  for sin, because they have not believed in me; and for righteousness, because I go  to my Father; and for judgement, because the Archon of this world hath been  judged.

[47:59] And further have I many things to speak unto you, but ye cannot tarry  now.

[47:60] Howbeit when the Spirit of truth is come, he will remind you of all the truth: he will say nothing from himself; but everything that he heareth, that shall  he say: and he shall make known unto you the things that are to be.

[47:61] And he shall  glorify me; for from me shall he take and shew you.

[47:62] All that my Father hath is mine: therefore said I unto you, that he taketh of mine, and shall shew you.

[48:1] Section XLVII.

[48:2] A little while, and ye shall not behold me; and a little while again, and ye shall  behold me; because I go to the Father.

[48:3] His disciples therefore said one to another, What is this that he hath said unto us, A little while, and ye shall not behold me; and a little while again, and ye shall behold me: and, I go to my  Father? And they said, What is this little while that he hath said? We know not  what he speaketh.

[48:4] And Jesus perceived that they were seeking to ask him, and said unto them, Do ye inquire among yourselves concerning this, that I said unto you, A little while, and ye behold me not, and a little while again, and ye shall  behold me? Verily, verily, I say unto you, that ye shall weep and grieve, but the world shall rejoice: and ye shall be sorrowful, but your grief shall turn to joy.

[48:5] For, a woman when the time is come for her that she should bring forth, the arrival of the day of her bringing forth distresseth her: but whenever she hath brought forth a son, she remembereth not her distress, for joy at the birth of a man into the  world.

[48:6] And ye now also grieve: but I shall see you, and your hearts shall rejoice,  Arabic, p.

[48:7] and your joy no man taketh from you.

[48:8] And in that day ye shall ask me nothing.

[48:9] And verily, verily, I say unto you, All that ye ask my Father in my name, he will give you.

[48:10] Hitherto ye have asked nothing  in my name: ask, and ye shall receive, that your joy may be complete.

[48:11] I have spoken unto you now in aenigmas: but there will come an hour when I shall not speak to you in aenigmas, but shall reveal unto you the Father plainly,  in that day when ye shall ask in my name: and I say not unto you, that I shall  entreat the Father for you; for the Father loveth you, because ye have loved me,  and have believed that I came forth from my Father.

[48:12] I came forth from my Father, and came into the world: and I leave the world, and go unto my Father.

[48:13] His disciples said unto him, Lo, thy speech is now plain, and thou hast not said one  thing in an aenigma.

[48:14] Now, lo, we know that thou knowest everything, and needest not that any man should ask thee: and by this we believe that thou camest forth ,  from God.

[48:15] Jesus said unto them, Believe that an hour cometh, and lo, it hath come, and ye shall be scattered, every one of you to his place, and shall leave me  alone: and yet I am not alone, because the Father is with me.

[48:16] This have I said unto you, that in me ye may have peace.

[48:17] And in the world trouble shall overtake you: but be of good courage; for I have overcome the world.

[48:18] This said Jesus, and lifted up his eyes unto heaven, and said, My Father, the hour  is come; glorify thy Son, that thy Son may glorify thee: as thou gavest him authority  over all flesh, that all that thou hast given him, he might give them eternal life.

[48:19] And this is eternal life, that they should know that thou alone art true God, and that he  Arabic, p.

[48:20] whom thou didst send is Jesus the Messiah.

[48:21] I glorified thee in the earth,  and the work which thou gavest me to do I have accomplished.

[48:22] And now glorify thou me, O Father, beside thee, with that glory which I had with thee  before the world was.

[48:23] I made known thy name to the men whom thou gavest me out of the world: thine they were, and thou gavest them to me; and they have kept ,  thy word.

[48:24] Now they know that all that thou hast given me is from thee: and the sayings which thou gavest me I have given unto them; and they received them, and knew of a truth that I came forth from thee, and believed that thou didst send me.

[48:25] And I ask for their sake: and my asking is not for the world, but for those whom  thou hast given me; for they are thine: and all that is mine is thine, and all that is  thine is mine: and I am glorified in them.

[48:26] And now I am not in the world, and they are in the world, and I come to thee.

[48:27] My holy Father, keep them in thy  name which thou hast given unto me, that they may be one, as we are.

[48:28] When I was with them in the world, I kept them in thy name: and I kept those whom thou gavest unto me: and no man of them hath perished, but the son of perdition; that  the scripture might be fulfilled.

[48:29] Now I come to thee: and this I say in the world,  that my joy may be complete in them.

[48:30] I have given them thy word; and the world  hated them, because they were not of the world, as I was not of the world.

[48:31] And I ask not this, that thou take them from the world, but that thou keep them from the ,  evil one.

[48:32] They were not of the world, as I was not of the world.

[48:33] O Father, sanctify  them in thy truth: for thy word is truth.

[48:34] And as thou didst send me into the world, I  Arabic, p.

[48:35] also send them into the world.

[48:36] And for their sake I sanctify myself, that they  also may be sanctified in the truth.

[48:37] Neither for these alone do I ask, but for  the sake of them that believe in me through their word; that they may be all one; as thou art in me, and I in thee, and so they also shall be one in us: that the world  may believe that thou didst send me.

[48:38] And the glory which thou hast given unto  me I have given unto them; that they may be one, as we are one; I in them, and thou in me, that they may be perfect into one; and that the world may know that  thou didst send me, and that I loved them, as thou lovedst me.

[48:39] Father, and those whom thou hast given me, I wish that, where I am, they may be with me also; that they may behold my glory, which thou hast given me: for thou lovedst me before  the foundation of the world.

[48:40] My righteous Father, and the world knew thee not,  but I know thee; and they knew that thou didst send me; and I made known unto them thy name, and will make it known to them; that the love wherewith thou lovedst me may be in them, and I shall be in them.

[49:1] Section XLVIII.

[49:2] This said Jesus, and went forth with his disciples to a place which was called Gethsemane, on the side that is in the plain of Kidron, the mountain, the place  in which was a garden; and he entered thither, he and his disciples.

[49:3] And Judas the  betrayer knew that place: for Jesus oft-times met with his disciples there.

[49:4] And when Jesus came to the place, he said to his disciples, Sit ye here, so that I may go and pray; ,  Arabic, p.

[49:5] and pray ye, that ye enter not into temptations.

[49:6] And he took with him Cephas and the sons of Zebedee together, James and John; and he began to  look sorrowful, and to be anxious.

[49:7] And he said unto them, My soul is distressed unto  death: abide ye here, and watch with me.

[49:8] And he withdrew from them a little,  the space of a stone's throw; and he kneeled, and fell on his face, and prayed, so  that, if it were possible, this hour might pass him.

[49:9] And he said, Father, thou art able for all things; if thou wilt, let this cup pass me: but let not my will be done,  but let thy will be done.

[49:10] And he came to his disciples, and found them sleeping;  and he said unto Cephas, Simon, didst thou sleep? Could ye thus not for one hour  watch with me? Watch and pray, that ye enter not into temptations: the spirit is  willing and ready, but the body is weak.

[49:11] And he went again a second time, and prayed, and said, My Father, if it is not possible with regard to this cup that it pass,  except I drink it, thy will be done.

[49:12] And he returned again, and found his disciples sleeping, for their eyes were heavy from their grief and anxiety; and they knew not  what to say to him.

[49:13] And he left them, and went away again, and prayed a third  time, and said the very same word.

[49:14] And there appeared unto him an angel from  heaven, encouraging him.

[49:15] And being afraid he prayed continuously: and his sweat  Arabic, p.

[49:16] became like a stream of blood, and fell on the ground.

[49:17] Then he rose from  his prayer, and came to his disciples, and found them sleeping.

[49:18] And he  said unto them, Sleep now, and rest: the end hath arrived, and the hour hath come;  and behold, the Son of man is betrayed into the hands of sinners.

[49:19] Arise, let us go: for he hath come that betrayeth me.

[49:20] And while he was still speaking, came Judas the betrayer, one of the twelve, and with him a great multitude carrying lanterns and torches and swords and staves, from the chief priests and scribes and elders of the people, and with him the footsoldiers  of the Romans.

[49:21] And Judas the betrayer gave them a sign, and said, He whom I shall kiss, he is he: take him with care, and lead him away.

[49:22] And Jesus, because he knew everything that should come upon him, went forth  unto them.

[49:23] And immediately Judas the betrayer came to Jesus, and said, Peace,  my Master; and kissed him.

[49:24] And Jesus said unto him, Judas, with a kiss betrayest  thou the Son of man? Was it for that thou camest, my friend? And Jesus said  to those that came unto him, Whom seek ye? They said unto him, Jesus the Nazarene.

[49:25] Jesus said unto them, I am he.

[49:26] And Judas the betrayer also was standing  with them.

[49:27] And when Jesus said unto them, I am he, they retreated backward, and  fell to the ground.

[49:28] And Jesus asked them again, Whom seek ye? They answered,  Jesus the Nazarene.

[49:29] Jesus said unto them, I told you that I am he: and if ye seek  me, let these go away: that the word might be fulfilled which he spake, Of those  Arabic, p.

[49:30] whom thou hast given me I lost not even one.

[49:31] Then came those that were with Judas, and seized Jesus, and took him.

[49:32] And when his disciples saw what happened, they said, Our Lord, shall we smite  them with swords? And Simon Cephas had a sword, and he drew it, and struck the servant of the chief priest, and cut off his right ear.

[49:33] And the name of that servant  was Malchus.

[49:34] Jesus said unto Cephas, The cup which my Father hath given  me, shall I not drink it? Put the sword into its sheath: for all that take with the  sword shall die by the sword.

[49:35] Thinkest thou that I am not able to ask of my  Father, and he shall now raise up for me more than twelve tribes of angels? Then  how should the scriptures which were spoken be fulfilled, that thus it must be? Your  leave in this.

[49:36] And he touched the ear of him that was struck, and healed it.

[49:37] And in that hour Jesus said to the multitudes, As they come out against a thief are ye come out against me with swords and staves to take me? Daily was I with you in  the temple sitting teaching, and ye took me not: but this is your hour, and the power  of darkness.

[49:38] And that was, that the scriptures of the prophets might be fulfilled.

[49:39] Then the disciples all left him, and fled.

[49:40] And the footsoldiers and the officers  and the soldiers of the Jews seized Jesus, and came.

[49:41] And a certain young man  followed him, and he was wrapped in a towel, naked: and they seized him; so he  Arabic, p.

[49:42] left the towel, and fled naked.

[49:43] Then they took Jesus, and bound him, and brought him to Annas first; because he was the father in law of Caiaphas,  who was chief priest that year.

[49:44] And Caiaphas was he that counselled the Jews, that it was necessary that one man should die instead of the people.

[49:45] And Simon Cephas and one of the other disciples followed Jesus.

[49:46] And the chief  priest knew that disciple, and he entered with Jesus into the court; but Simon was standing without at the door.

[49:47] And that other disciple, whom the chief priest knew,  went out and spake unto her that kept the door, and she brought Simon in.

[49:48] And when the maid that kept the door saw Simon, she looked stedfastly at him, and said unto him, Art not thou also one of the disciples of this man, I mean Jesus the  Nazarene? But he denied, and said, Woman, I know him not, neither know I even  what thou sayest.

[49:49] And the servants and the soldiers rose, and made a fire in the  middle of the court, that they might warm themselves; for it was cold.

[49:50] And when  the fire burned up, they sat down around it.

[49:51] And Simon also came, and sat down with them to warm himself, that he might see the end of what should happen.

[50:1] Section XLIX.

[50:2] ,  And the chief priest asked Jesus about his disciples, and about his doctrine.

[50:3] And Jesus said unto him, I was speaking openly to the people; and I ever taught in the synagogue, and in the temple, where all the Jews gather; and I have spoken nothing in  Arabic, p.

[50:4] secret.

[50:5] Why askest thou me? ask those that have heard, what I spake unto  them: for they know all that I said.

[50:6] And when he had said that, one of the soldiers which were standing there struck the cheek of Jesus, and said unto him,  Dost thou thus answer the chief priest? Jesus answered and said unto him, If I  have spoken evil, bear witness of evil: but if well, why didst thou smite me? And Annas sent Jesus bound unto Caiaphas the chief priest.

[50:7] And when Jesus went out, Simon Cephas was standing in the outer court warming  himself.

[50:8] And that maid saw him again, and began to say to those that stood  by, This man also was there with Jesus the Nazarene.

[50:9] And those that stood by  came forward and said to Cephas, Truly thou art one of his disciples.

[50:10] And he  denied again with an oath, I know not the man.

[50:11] And after a little one of the servants of the chief priest, the kinsman of him whose ear Simon cut off, saw him; and  he disputed and said, Truly this man was with him: and he also is a Galilaean;  and his speech resembles.

[50:12] And he said unto Simon, Did not I see thee with him  in the garden? Then began Simon to curse, and to swear, I know not this man  whom ye have mentioned.

[50:13] And immediately, while he was speaking, the cock crew  twice.

[50:14] And in that hour Jesus turned, he being without, and looked stedfastly at Cephas.

[50:15] And Simon remembered the word of our Lord, which he said unto him, ,  Before the cock crow twice, thou shalt deny me thrice.

[50:16] And Simon went forth without, and wept bitterly.

[50:17] Arabic, p.

[50:18] And when the morning approached, the servants of all the chief priests and the scribes and the elders of the people and all the multitude assembled, ,  and made a plot; and they took counsel against Jesus to put him to death.

[50:19] And they sought false witnesses who should witness against him, that they might put him to ,  death, and they found not; but many false witnesses came, but their witness did not ,  agree.

[50:20] But at last there came two lying witnesses, and said, We heard him say, I will destroy this temple of God that is made with hands, and will build another not ,  made with hands after three days.

[50:21] And not even so did their witness agree.

[50:22] But Jesus was silent.

[50:23] And the chief priest rose in the midst, and asked Jesus, and said,  Answerest thou not a word concerning anything? what do these witness against ,  thee? But Jesus was silent, and answered him nothing.

[50:24] And they took him up  into their assembly, and said unto him, If thou art the Messiah, tell us.

[50:25] He said  unto them, If I tell you, ye will not believe me: and if I ask you, ye will not answer  me a word, nor let me go.

[50:26] And the chief priest answered and said unto him, I adjure thee by the living God, that thou tell us whether thou art the Messiah, the ,  Son of the living God.

[50:27] Jesus said unto him, Thou hast said that I am he.

[50:28] They all said unto him, Then thou art now the Son of God? Jesus said, Ye have said  that I am he.

[50:29] I say unto you, that henceforth ye shall see the Son of man sitting  Arabic, p.

[50:30] at the right hand of power, and coming on the clouds of heaven.

[50:31] Then the  chief priest rent his tunic, and said, He hath blasphemed.

[50:32] And they all said, Why should we seek now witnesses? we have heard now the blasphemy from his mouth.

[50:33] ,  What then think ye? They all answered and said, He is worthy of death.

[50:34] Then some of them drew near, and spat in his face, and struck him, and scoffed at him.

[50:35] And the soldiers struck him on his cheeks, and said, Prophesy unto us, thou Messiah:  who is he that struck thee? And many other things spake they falsely, and said against him.

[50:36] And all of their assembly arose, and took Jesus, and brought him bound to  the praetorium, and delivered him up to Pilate the judge; but they entered not into the praetorium, that they might not be defiled when they should eat the passover.

[50:37] And Jesus stood before the judge.

[50:38] And Pilate went forth unto them without, and  said unto them, What accusation have ye against this man? They answered and said unto him, If he had not been doing evils, neither should we have delivered  him up unto thee.

[50:39] We found this man leading our people astray, and restraining from giving tribute to Caesar, and saying of himself that he is the King, the Messiah.

[50:40] Pilate said unto them, Then take ye him, and judge him according to your law.

[50:41] Arabic, p.

[50:42] The Jews said unto him, We have no authority to put a man to death:  that the word might be fulfilled, which Jesus spake, when he made known by what manner of death he was to die.

[50:43] And Pilate entered into the praetorium, and called Jesus, and said unto him, Art  thou the King of the Jews? Jesus said unto him, Of thyself saidst thou this, or  did others tell it thee concerning me? Pilate said unto him, Am I, forsooth, a Jew? The sons of thy nation and the chief priests delivered thee unto me: what  hast thou done? Jesus said unto him, My kingdom is not of this world: if my kingdom were of this world, then would my servants fight, that I should not be  delivered to the Jews: now my kingdom is not from hence.

[50:44] Pilate said unto him, Then thou art a king? Jesus said unto him, Thou hast said that I am a king.

[50:45] And for this was I born, and for this came I into the world, that I should bear witness  of the truth.

[50:46] And every one that is of the truth heareth my voice.

[50:47] Pilate said unto him, And what is the truth? And when he said that, he went out again unto the Jews.

[51:1] Section L.

[51:2] And Pilate said unto the chief priests and the multitude, I have not found  against this man anything.

[51:3] But they cried out and said, He hath disquieted our people with his teaching in all Judaea, and he began from Galilee and unto this  place.

[51:4] And Pilate, when he heard the name of Galilee, asked, Is this man a Galilaean?  And when he learned that he was under the jurisdiction of Herod, he sent him to Herod: for he was in Jerusalem in those days.

[51:5] And Herod, when he saw Jesus, rejoiced exceedingly: for he had desired to see him for a long time, because he had heard regarding him many things; and he counted on  Arabic, p.

[51:6] seeing some sign from him.

[51:7] And he questioned him with many words; but  Jesus answered him not a word.

[51:8] And the scribes and chief priests were  standing by, and they accused him vehemently.

[51:9] And Herod scoffed at him, he and his servants; and when he had scoffed at him, he clothed him in robes of scarlet,  and sent him to Pilate.

[51:10] And on that day Pilate and Herod became friends, there having been enmity between them before that.

[51:11] ,  And Pilate called the chief priests and the rulers of the people, and said unto them, Ye brought unto me this man, as the perverter of your people: and I have tried him before you, and have not found in this man any cause of all that ye  seek against him: nor yet Herod: for I sent him unto him; and he hath done  nothing for which he should deserve death.

[51:12] So now I will chastise him, and let ,  him go.

[51:13] The multitude all cried out and said, Take him from us, take him.

[51:14] And  the chief priests and the elders accused him of many things.

[51:15] And during their  accusation he answered not a word.

[51:16] Then Pilate said unto him, Hearest thou not  how many things they witness against thee? And he answered him not, not even one word: and Pilate marvelled at that.

[51:17] And when the judge sat on his tribune, his wife sent unto him, and said unto him, See that thou have nothing to do with that righteous man: for I have suffered much in my dream to-day because of him.

[51:18] And at every feast the custom of the judge was to release to the people one  prisoner, him whom they would.

[51:19] And there was in their prison a well-known prisoner, ,  called Barabbas.

[51:20] And when they assembled, Pilate said unto them, Ye have a custom, that I should release unto you a prisoner at the passover: will ye that I  release unto you the King of the Jews? And they all cried out and said, Release not Arabic, p.

[51:21] unto us this man, but release unto us Barabbas.

[51:22] And this Barabbas was a  robber, who for sedition and murder, which was in the city, was cast into the  prison.

[51:23] And all the people cried out and began to ask him to do as the custom was  that he should do with them.

[51:24] And Pilate answered and said unto them, Whom will ye that I release unto you? Barabbas, or Jesus which is called the Messiah, the  King of the Jews? For Pilate knew that envy had moved them to deliver him up.

[51:25] And the chief priests and the elders asked the multitudes to deliver Barabbas, and  to destroy Jesus.

[51:26] The judge answered and said unto them, Whom of the two will  ye that I release unto you? They said, Barabbas.

[51:27] Pilate said unto them, And  Jesus which is called the Messiah, what shall I do with him? They all cried out  and said, Crucify him.

[51:28] And Pilate spake to them again, for he desired to release  Jesus; but they cried out and said, Crucify him, crucify him, and release unto us  Barabbas.

[51:29] And Pilate said unto them a third time, What evil hath this man done? I have not found in him any cause to necessitate death: I will chastise him and  let him go.

[51:30] But they increased in importunity with a loud voice, and asked him to crucify him.

[51:31] And their voice, and the voice of the chief priests, prevailed.

[51:32] Then Pilate released unto them that one who was cast into prison for sedition and murder, Barabbas, whom they asked for: and he scourged Jesus with whips.

[51:33] Then the footsoldiers of the judge took Jesus, and went into the praetorium, and  Arabic, p.

[51:34] gathered unto him all of the footsoldiers.

[51:35] And they stripped him, and put on  him a scarlet cloak.

[51:36] And they clothed him in garments of purple, and plaited  a crown of thorns, and placed it on his head, and a reed in his right hand; and while they mocked at him and laughed, they fell down on their knees before him, and bowed  down to him, and said, Hail, King of the Jews! And they spat in his face, and took the reed from his hand, and struck him on his head, and smote his cheeks.

[51:37] And Pilate went forth without again, and said unto the Jews, I bring him forth to  you, that ye may know that I do not find, in examining him, even one crime.

[51:38] And Jesus went forth without, wearing the crown of thorns and the purple garments.

[51:39] Pilate said unto them, Behold, the man! And when the chief priests and the soldiers saw him, they cried out and said, Crucify him, crucify him.

[51:40] Pilate said unto them, Take him yourselves, and crucify him: for I find not a cause against  him.

[51:41] The Jews said unto him, We have a law, and according to our law he deserves  death, because he made himself the Son of God.

[51:42] And when Pilate heard this word,  his fear increased; and he entered again into the porch, and said to Jesus, Whence  art thou? But Jesus answered him not a word.

[51:43] Pilate said unto him, Speakest thou not unto me? knowest thou not that I have authority to release thee, and have  authority to crucify thee? Jesus said unto him, Thou hast not any authority over me, if thou wert not given it from above: therefore the sin of him that delivered  me up unto thee is greater than thy sin.

[51:44] And for this word Pilate wished to release him: but the Jews cried out, If thou let him go, thou art not a friend of Caesar: for every one that maketh himself a king is against Caesar.

[52:1] Section LI.

[52:2] Arabic, p.

[52:3] And when Pilate heard this saying, he took Jesus out, and sat on the tribune in the place which was called the pavement of stones, but in the Hebrew  called Gabbatha.

[52:4] And that day was the Friday of the passover: and it had reached  about the sixth hour.

[52:5] And he said to the Jews, Behold, your King! And they cried out, Take him, take him, crucify him, crucify him.

[52:6] Pilate said unto them, Shall I crucify your King? The chief priests said unto him, We have no king except  Caesar.

[52:7] And Pilate, when he saw it, and he was gaining nothing, but the tumult was increasing, took water, and washed his hands before the multitude, and said, I  am innocent of the blood of this innocent man: ye shall know.

[52:8] And all the people  answered and said, His blood be on us, and on our children.

[52:9] Then Pilate commanded to grant them their request; and delivered up Jesus to be crucified, according to their wish.

[52:10] Then Judas the betrayer, when he saw Jesus wronged, went and returned the  thirty pieces of money to the chief priests and the elders, and said, I have sinned in my betraying innocent blood.

[52:11] And they said unto him, And we, what must we do?  know thou.

[52:12] And he threw down the money in the temple, and departed; and he  went away and hanged himself.

[52:13] And the chief priests took the money, and said, We have not authority to cast it into the place of the offering, for it is the price  of blood.

[52:14] And they took counsel, and bought with it the plain of the potter, for  the burial of strangers.

[52:15] Therefore that plain was called, The field of blood, unto  Arabic, p.

[52:16] this day.

[52:17] Therein was fulfilled the saying in the prophet which said, I took thirty pieces of money, the price of the precious one, which was fixed  by the children of Israel; and I paid them for the plain of the potter, as the Lord commanded me.

[52:18] And the Jews took Jesus, and went away to crucify him.

[52:19] And when he bare his  cross and went out, they stripped him of those purple and scarlet garments which he  had on, and put on him his own garments.

[52:20] And while they were going with him, they found a man, a Cyrenian, coming from the country, named Simon, the father of Alexander and Rufus: and they compelled this man to bear the cross of Jesus.

[52:21] And they took the cross and laid it upon him, that he might bear it, and come after Jesus; and Jesus went, and his cross behind him.

[52:22] And there followed him much people, and women which were lamenting and  raving.

[52:23] But Jesus turned unto them and said, Daughters of Jerusalem, weep not  for me: weep for yourselves, and for your children.

[52:24] Days are coming, when they shall say, Blessed are the barren, and the wombs that bare not, and the breasts  that gave not suck.

[52:25] Then shall they begin to say to the mountains, Fall on us; and  to the hills, Cover us.

[52:26] For if they do so in the green tree, what shall be in the dry?   And they brought with Jesus two others of the malefactors, to be put to death.

[52:27] And when they came unto a certain place called The skull, and called in the Hebrew Golgotha, they crucified him there: they crucified with him these two  malefactors, one on his right, and the other on his left.

[52:28] And the scripture was  Arabic, p.

[52:29] fulfilled, which saith, He was numbered with the transgressors.

[52:30] And they gave him to drink wine and myrrh, and vinegar which had been mixed with the myrrh; and he tasted, and would not drink; and he received it not.

[52:31] And the soldiers, when they had crucified Jesus, took his garments, and cast lots for them in four parts, to every party of the soldiers a part; and his tunic was  without sewing, from the top woven throughout.

[52:32] And they said one to another, Let us not rend it, but cast lots for it, whose it shall be: and the scripture was fulfilled, which saith,  They divided my garments among them,  And cast the lot for my vesture.

[52:33] ,  This the soldiers did.

[52:34] And they sat and guarded him there.

[52:35] And Pilate wrote on a tablet the cause of his death, and put it on the wood of the cross above his head.

[52:36] And there was written upon it thus: This is Jesus the Nazarene, the King of the  Jews.

[52:37] And this tablet read many of the Jews: for the place where Jesus was crucified was near the city: and it was written in Hebrew and Greek and Latin.

[52:38] And the chief priests said unto Pilate, Write not, The King of the Jews; but, He it is  that said, I am the King of the Jews.

[52:39] Pilate said unto them, What hath been  written hath been written.

[52:40] And the people were standing beholding; and they  that passed by were reviling him, and shaking their heads, and saying, Thou that destroyest the temple, and buildest it in three days, save thyself if thou art the Son  of God, and come down from the cross.

[52:41] And in like manner the chief priests and the Arabic, p.

[52:42] scribes and the elders and the Pharisees derided him, and laughed one with ,  another, and said, The saviour of others cannot save himself.

[52:43] If he is the Messiah, the chosen of God, and the King of Israel, let him come down now from the  cross, that we may see, and believe in him.

[52:44] He that relieth on God—let him deliver him  now, if he is pleased with him: for he said, I am the Son of God.

[52:45] And the soldiers  also scoffed at him in that they came near unto him, and brought him vinegar, and  said unto him, If thou art the King of the Jews, save thyself.

[52:46] And likewise the two robbers also that were crucified with him reproached him.

[52:47] And one of those two malefactors who were crucified with him reviled him, and  said, If thou art the Messiah, save thyself, and save us also.

[52:48] But his comrade rebuked him, and said, Dost thou not even fear God, being thyself also in this  condemnation? And we with justice, and as we deserved, and according to our deed, have we been rewarded: but this man hath not done anything unlawful.

[52:49] And he said unto Jesus, Remember me, my Lord, when thou comest in thy kingdom.

[52:50] Jesus said unto him, Verily I say unto thee, To-day shalt thou be with me in Paradise.

[52:51] And there stood by the cross of Jesus his mother, and his mother's sister,  Mary that was related to Clopas, and Mary Magdalene.

[52:52] And Jesus saw his mother, and that disciple whom he loved standing by; and he said to his mother,  Woman, behold, thy son! And he said to that disciple, Behold, thy mother! And from that hour that disciple took her unto himself.

[52:53] Arabic, p.

[52:54] And from the sixth hour darkness was on all the land unto the ninth  hour, and the sun became dark.

[52:55] And at the ninth hour Jesus cried out with a loud voice, and said, Yail, Yaili, why hast thou forsaken me? which is, My  God, my God, why hast thou forsaken me? And some of those that stood there, when they heard, said, This man called Elijah.

[53:1] Section LII.

[53:2] And after that, Jesus knew that all things were finished; and that the scripture  might be accomplished, he said, I thirst.

[53:3] And there was set a vessel full of vinegar: and in that hour one of them hasted, and took a sponge, and filled it with that  vinegar, and fastened it on a reed, and brought it near his mouth to give him a  drink.

[53:4] And when Jesus had taken that vinegar, he said, Everything is finished.

[53:5] But the rest said, Let be, that we may see whether Elijah cometh to save him.

[53:6] ,  And Jesus said, My Father, forgive them; for they know not what they do.

[53:7] And Jesus cried again with a loud voice, and said, My Father, into thy hands I commend my spirit.

[53:8] He said that, and bowed his head, and gave up his spirit.

[53:9] And immediately the face of the door of the temple was rent into two parts from  top to bottom; and the earth was shaken; and the stones were split to pieces; and the Arabic, p.

[53:10] tombs were opened; and the bodies of many saints which slept, arose and  came forth; and after his resurrection they entered into the holy city and  appeared unto many.

[53:11] And the officer of the footsoldiers, and they that were with him who were guarding Jesus, when they saw the earthquake, and the things which came  to pass, feared greatly, and praised God, and said, This man was righteous; and,  Truly he was the Son of God.

[53:12] And all the multitudes that were come together to the sight, when they saw what came to pass, returned and smote upon their breasts.

[53:13] And the Jews, because of the Friday, said, Let these bodies not remain on their crosses, because it is the morning of the sabbath (for that sabbath was a great day); and they asked of Pilate that they might break the legs of those that were  crucified, and take them down.

[53:14] And the soldiers came, and brake the legs of the  first, and that other which was crucified with him: but when they came to Jesus,  they saw that he had died before, so they brake not his legs: but one of the soldiers pierced him in his side with a spear, and immediately there came forth blood and  water.

[53:15] And he that hath seen hath borne witness, and his witness is true: and he  knoweth that he hath said the truth, that ye also may believe.

[53:16] This he did, that  the scripture might be fulfilled, which saith, A bone shall not be broken in him; and the scripture also which saith, Let them look upon him whom they pierced.

[53:17] And there were in the distance all the acquaintance of Jesus standing, and the women that came with him from Galilee, those that followed him and ministered.

[53:18] One of them was Mary Magdalene; and Mary the mother of James the little and  Arabic, p.

[53:19] Joses, and the mother of the sons of Zebedee, and Salome, and many others which came up with him unto Jerusalem; and they saw that.

[53:20] And when the evening of the Friday was come, because of the entering of the  sabbath, there came a rich man, a noble of Ramah, a city of Judah, named Joseph, and he was a good man and upright; and he was a disciple of Jesus, but  was concealing himself for fear of the Jews.

[53:21] And he did not agree with the accusers  in their desire and their deeds: and he was looking for the kingdom of God.

[53:22] And this man went boldly, and entered in unto Pilate, and asked of him the body of  Jesus.

[53:23] And Pilate wondered how he had died already: and he called the officer of  the footsoldiers, and asked him concerning his death before the time.

[53:24] And when  he knew, he commanded him to deliver up his body unto Joseph.

[53:25] And Joseph bought for him a winding cloth of pure linen, and took down the body of Jesus,  and wound it in it; and they came and took it.

[53:26] And there came unto him Nicodemus also, who of old came unto Jesus by night; and he brought with him perfume  of myrrh and aloes, about a hundred pounds.

[53:27] And they took the body of Jesus, and wound it in the linen and the perfume, as was the custom of the Jews to bury.

[53:28] And there was in the place where Jesus was crucified a garden; and in that garden  a new tomb cut out in a rock, wherein was never man yet laid.

[53:29] And they left  Jesus there because the sabbath had come in, and because the tomb was near.

[53:30] And they pushed a great stone, and thrust it against the door of the sepulchre, and  went away.

[53:31] And Mary Magdalene and Mary that was related to Joses came to  Arabic, p.

[53:32] the sepulchre after them, and sat opposite the sepulchre, and saw the  body, how they took it in and laid it there.

[53:33] And they returned, and bought ointment and perfume, and prepared it, that they might come and anoint him.

[53:34] And on the day which was the sabbath day they desisted according to the command.

[53:35] ,  And the chief priests and the Pharisees gathered unto Pilate, and said unto him, Our lord, we remember that that misleader said, while he was alive, After three days  I rise.

[53:36] And now send beforehand and guard the tomb until the third day, lest his disciples come and steal him by night, and they will say unto the people that he  is risen from the dead: and the last error shall be worse than the first.

[53:37] He said unto them, And have ye not guards? go, and take precautions as ye know how.

[53:38] And they went, and set guards at the tomb, and sealed that stone, with the guards.

[53:39] And in the evening of the sabbath, which is the morning of the first day, and in  the dawning while the darkness yet remained, came Mary Magdalene and the other Mary and other women to see the tomb.

[53:40] They brought with them the  perfume which they had prepared, and said among themselves, Who is it that will  remove for us the stone from the door of the tomb? for it was very great.

[53:41] And when they said thus, there occurred a great earthquake; and an angel came down  from heaven, and came and removed the stone from the door.

[53:42] And they came and found the stone removed from the sepulchre, and the angel sitting upon the  stone.

[53:43] And his appearance was as the lightning, and his raiment white as the  snow: and for fear of him the guards were troubled, and became as dead men.

[53:44] And when he went away, the women entered into the sepulchre; and they found  Arabic, p.

[53:45] not the body of Jesus.

[53:46] And they saw there a young man sitting on the  right, arrayed in a white garment; and they were amazed.

[53:47] And the angel answered and said unto the women, Fear ye not: for I know that ye seek Jesus the  Nazarene, who hath been crucified.

[53:48] He is not here; but he is risen, as he said.

[53:49] Come and see the place where our Lord lay.

[54:1] Section LIII.

[54:2] And while they marvelled at that, behold, two men standing above them, their  raiment shining: and they were seized with fright, and bowed down their face to  the earth: and they said unto them, Why seek ye the living one with the dead? He is not here; he is risen: remember what he was speaking unto you while he was in  Galilee, and saying, The Son of man is to be delivered up into the hands of sinners,  and to be crucified, and on the third day to rise.

[54:3] But go in haste, and say to his disciples and to Cephas, He is risen from among the dead; and lo, he goeth before  you into Galilee; and there ye shall see him, where he said unto you: lo, I have  told you.

[54:4] And they remembered his sayings; and they departed in haste from the  tomb with joy and great fear, and hastened and went; and perplexity and fear  encompassed them; and they told no man anything, for they were afraid.

[54:5] And Mary hastened, and came to Simon Cephas, and to that other disciple whom Jesus loved, and said unto them, They have taken our Lord from the sepulchre, and I  know not where they have laid him.

[54:6] And Simon went out, and that other disciple,  and came to the sepulchre.

[54:7] And they hastened both together: and that disciple  outran Simon, and came first to the sepulchre; and he looked down, and saw the  linen laid; but he went not in.

[54:8] And Simon came after him, and entered into the  Arabic, p.

[54:9] sepulchre, and saw the linen laid; and the scarf with which his head was bound was not with the linen, but wrapped and laid aside in a certain place.

[54:10] Then entered that disciple which came first to the sepulchre, and saw, and believed.

[54:11] And they knew not yet from the scriptures that the Messiah was to rise from among  the dead.

[54:12] And those two disciples went to their place.

[54:13] But Mary remained at the tomb weeping: and while she wept, she looked  down into the tomb; and she saw two angels sitting in white raiment, one of them toward his pillow, and the other toward his feet, where the body of Jesus had been  laid.

[54:14] And they said unto her, Woman, why weepest thou? She said unto them,  They have taken my Lord, and I know not where they have left him.

[54:15] She said that, and turned behind her, and saw Jesus standing, and knew not that it was  Jesus.

[54:16] Jesus said unto her, Woman, why weepest thou? whom seekest thou? And she supposed him to be the gardener, and said, My lord, if thou hast taken him,  tell me where thou hast laid him, that I may go and take him.

[54:17] Jesus said unto her, Mary.

[54:18] She turned, and said unto him in Hebrew, Rabboni; which is, being  interpreted, Teacher.

[54:19] Jesus said unto her, Touch me not; for I have not ascended yet unto my Father: go to my brethren, and say unto them, I ascend unto my Father and your Father, and my God and your God.

[54:20] And on the First-day on which he rose, he appeared first unto Mary Magdalene, from whom he had cast out seven demons.

[54:21] And some of those guards came to the city, and informed the chief priests of  Arabic, p.

[54:22] all that had happened.

[54:23] And they assembled with the elders, and took  counsel; and they gave money, not a little, to the guards, and said unto them, Say ye, His disciples came and stole him by night, while we were sleeping.

[54:24] And if the judge hear that, we will make a plea with him, and free you of blame.

[54:25] And they, when they took the money, did according to what they taught them.

[54:26] And this word spread among the Jews unto this day.

[54:27] And then came Mary Magdalene, and announced to the disciples that she had seen our Lord, and that he had said that unto her.

[54:28] And while the first women were going in the way to inform his disciples,  Jesus met them, and said unto them, Peace unto you.

[54:29] And they came and took  hold of his feet, and worshipped him.

[54:30] Then said Jesus unto them, Fear not: but go and say to my brethren that they depart into Galilee, and there they shall see  me.

[54:31] And those women returned, and told all that to the eleven, and to the rest of the disciples; and to those that had been with him, for they were saddened and  weeping.

[54:32] And those were Mary Magdalene, and Joanna, and Mary the mother of James, and the rest who were with them: and they were those that told the apostles.

[54:33] And they, when they heard them say that he was alive and had appeared unto them,  did not believe them: and these sayings were before their eyes as the sayings of madness.

[54:34] Arabic, p.

[54:35] And after that, he appeared to two of them, on that day, and while they were going to the village which was named Emmaus, and whose distance  from Jerusalem was sixty furlongs.

[54:36] And they were talking the one of them with the  other of all the things which had happened.

[54:37] And during the time of their talking and  inquiring with one another, Jesus came and reached them, and walked with them.

[54:38] But  their eyes were veiled that they should not know him.

[54:39] And he said unto them, What are these sayings which ye address the one of you to the other, as ye walk and are  sad? One of them, whose name was Cleopas, answered and said unto him, Art thou perchance alone a stranger to Jerusalem, since thou knowest not what was in  it in these days? He said unto them, What was? They said unto him, Concerning Jesus, he who was from Nazareth, a man who was a prophet, and powerful in  speech and deeds before God and before all the people: and the chief priests and  the elders delivered him up to the sentence of death, and crucified him.

[54:40] But we supposed that he was the one who was to deliver Israel.

[54:41] And since all these  things happened there have passed three days.

[54:42] But certain women of us also  informed us that they had come to the sepulchre; and when they found not his body, they came and told us that they had seen there the angels, and they said  concerning him that he was alive.

[54:43] And some of us also went to the sepulchre, and  found the matter as the women had said: only they saw him not.

[54:44] Then said Jesus  unto them, Ye lacking in discernment, and heavy in heart to believe! Was it not in all the sayings of the prophets that the Messiah was to suffer these things, and to  Arabic, p.

[54:45] enter into his Glory? And he began from Moses and from all the prophets,  and interpreted to them concerning himself from all the scriptures.

[54:46] And they drew near unto the village, whither they were going: and he was leading them to  imagine that he was as if going to a distant region.

[54:47] And they pressed him, and said unto him, Abide with us: for the day hath declined now to the darkness.

[54:48] And he went  in to abide with them.

[54:49] And when he sat with them, he took bread, and blessed,  and brake, and gave to them.

[54:50] And straightway their eyes were opened, and they  knew him; and he was taken away from them.

[54:51] And they said the one to the other, Was not our heart heavy within us, while he was speaking to us in the way, and interpreting to us the scriptures?   And they rose in that hour, and returned to Jerusalem, and found the eleven  gathered, and those that were with them, saying, Truly our Lord is risen, and hath  appeared to Simon.

[54:52] And they related what happened in the way, and how they knew him when he brake the bread.

[54:53] Neither believed they that also.

[55:1] Section LIV.

[55:2] And while they talked together, the evening of that day arrived which was the First-day; and the doors were shut where the disciples were, because of the fear of the  Jews; and Jesus came and stood among them, and said unto them, Peace be with you: I am he; fear not.

[55:3] But they were agitated, and became afraid, and supposed that they  saw a spirit.

[55:4] Jesus said unto them, Why are ye agitated? and why do thoughts rise  Arabic, p.

[55:5] in your hearts? See my hands and my feet, that I am he: feel me, and know that a spirit hath not flesh and bones, as ye see me having that.

[55:6] And when he had said this, he shewed them his hands and his feet and his side.

[55:7] And they were until this time unbelieving, from their joy and their wonder.

[55:8] He  said unto them, Have ye anything here to eat? And they gave him a portion of broiled fish and of honey.

[55:9] And he took it, and ate before them.

[55:10] And he said unto them, These are the sayings which I spake unto you, while I was with you, that everything must be fulfilled, which is written in the law of  Moses, and the prophets, and the psalms, concerning me.

[55:11] Then opened he their  heart, that they might understand the scriptures; and he said unto them, Thus it is written, and thus it is necessary that the Messiah suffer, and rise from among the  dead on the third day; and that repentance unto the forgiveness of sins be preached  in his name among all the peoples; and the beginning shall be from Jerusalem.

[55:12] And  ye shall be witnesses of that.

[55:13] And I send unto you the promise of my Father.

[55:14] And  when the disciples heard that, they were glad.

[55:15] And Jesus said unto them again,  Peace be with you: as my Father hath sent me, I also send you.

[55:16] And when he had said this, he breathed on them, and said unto them, Receive ye the Holy Spirit:  and if ye forgive sins to any man, they shall be forgiven him; and if ye retain them against any man, they shall be retained.

[55:17] But Thomas, one of the twelve, called Thama, was not there with the disciples  when Jesus came.

[55:18] The disciples therefore said unto him, We have seen our Lord.

[55:19] But he said unto them, If I do not see in his hands the places of the nails, and put on them my fingers, and pass my hand over his side, I will not believe.

[55:20] And after eight days, on the next First-day, the disciples were assembled again within, and Thomas with them.

[55:21] And Jesus came, the doors being shut, and stood  Arabic, p.

[55:22] in the midst, and said unto them, Peace be with you.

[55:23] And he said to Thomas, Bring hither thy finger, and behold my hands; and bring hither  thy hand, and spread it on my side: and be not unbelieving, but believing.

[55:24] Thomas  answered and said unto him, My Lord and my God.

[55:25] Jesus said unto him, Now since thou hast seen me, thou hast believed: blessed are they that have not seen me, and have believed.

[55:26] And many other signs did Jesus before his disciples, and they are they which  are not written in this book: but these that are written also are that ye may believe in Jesus the Messiah, the Son of God; and that when ye have believed, ye may have in his name eternal life.

[55:27] And after that, Jesus shewed himself again to his disciples at the sea of Tiberias;  and he shewed himself unto them thus.

[55:28] And there were together Simon Cephas, and Thomas which was called Twin, and Nathanael who was of Cana of Galilee,  and the sons of Zebedee, and two other of the disciples.

[55:29] Simon Cephas said unto them, I go to catch fish.

[55:30] They said unto him, And we also come with thee.

[55:31] And they went forth, and went up into the boat; and in that night they caught nothing.

[55:32] And when the morning arrived, Jesus stood on the shore of the sea: but the disciples  knew not that it was Jesus.

[55:33] And Jesus said unto them, Children, have ye anything  to eat? They said unto him, No.

[55:34] He said unto them, Cast your net from the right side of the boat, and ye shall find.

[55:35] And they threw, and they were not able  to draw the net for the abundance of the fish that were come into it.

[55:36] And that disciple whom Jesus loved said to Cephas, This is our Lord.

[55:37] And Simon, when he heard that it was our Lord, took his tunic, and girded it on his waist (for he was  naked), and cast himself into the sea to come to Jesus.

[55:38] But some others of the disciples came in the boat (and they were not far from the land, but about two  Arabic, p.

[55:39] hundred cubits), and drew that net of fish.

[55:40] And when they went up on the  land, they saw live coals laid, and fish laid thereon, and bread.

[55:41] And Jesus  said unto them, Bring of this fish which ye have now caught.

[55:42] Simon Cephas therefore went up, and dragged the net to the land, full of great fish, a hundred and fifty-three  fishes: and with all this weight that net was not rent.

[55:43] And Jesus said unto them, Come and sit down.

[55:44] And no man of the disciples dared to ask him who he was, for they knew that it was our Lord.

[55:45] But he did not appear to them in his own ,  form.

[55:46] And Jesus came, and took bread and fish, and gave unto them.

[55:47] This is the third time that Jesus appeared to his disciples, when he had risen from among the dead.

[55:48] And when they had breakfasted, Jesus said to Simon Cephas, Simon, son of Jonah, lovest thou me more than these? He said unto him, Yea, my Lord; thou  knowest that I love thee.

[55:49] Jesus said unto him, Feed for me my lambs.

[55:50] He said unto him again a second time, Simon, son of Jonah, lovest thou me? He said unto him, Yea, my Lord; thou knowest that I love thee.

[55:51] He said unto him, Feed for  me my sheep.

[55:52] He said unto him again the third time, Simon, son of Jonah, lovest thou me? And it grieved Cephas that he said unto him three times, Lovest thou me? He said unto him, My Lord, thou knowest everything; thou knowest that I  love thee.

[55:53] Jesus said unto him, Feed for me my sheep.

[55:54] Verily, verily, I say unto thee, When thou wast a child, thou didst gird thy waist for thyself, and go whither Arabic, p.

[55:55] thou wouldest: but when thou shalt be old, thou shalt stretch out thy hands, and another shall gird thy waist, and take thee whither thou wouldest not.

[55:56] He said that to him to explain by what death he was to glorify God.

[55:57] And when he  had said that, he said unto him, Come after me.

[55:58] And Simon Cephas turned, and saw that disciple whom Jesus loved following him; he which at the supper leaned on  Jesus' breast, and said, My Lord, who is it that betrayeth thee? When therefore Cephas saw him, he said to Jesus, My Lord, and this man, what shall be in his  case? Jesus said unto him, If I will that this man remain until I come, what is  that to thee? follow thou me.

[55:59] And this word spread among the brethren, that that disciple should not die: but Jesus said not that he should not die; but, If I will that this man remain until I come, what is that to thee?   This is the disciple which bare witness of that, and wrote it: and we know that his witness is true.

[56:1] Section LV.

[56:2] But the eleven disciples went into Galilee, to the mountain where Jesus had  appointed them.

[56:3] And when they saw him, they worshipped him: but there were of  them who doubted.

[56:4] And while they sat there he appeared to them again, and upbraided them for their lack of faith and the hardness of their hearts, those that saw him when he was risen, and believed not.

[56:5] Arabic, p.

[56:6] Then said Jesus unto them, I have been given all authority in heaven  and earth; and as my Father hath sent me, so I also send you.

[56:7] Go now into  all the world, and preach my gospel in all the creation; and teach all the peoples, and  baptize them in the name of the Father and the Son and the Holy Spirit; and teach them to keep all whatsoever I commanded you: and lo, I am with you all the days, unto  the end of the world.

[56:8] For whosoever believeth and is baptized shall be saved; but  whosoever believeth not shall be rejected.

[56:9] And the signs which shall attend those that believe in me are these: that they shall cast out devils in my name; and they  shall speak with new tongues; and they shall take up serpents, and if they drink deadly poison, it shall not injure them; and they shall lay their hands on the diseased,  and they shall be healed.

[56:10] But ye, abide in the city of Jerusalem, until ye be clothed with power from on high.

[56:11] And our Lord Jesus, after speaking to them, took them out to Bethany: and he  lifted up his hands, and blessed them.

[56:12] And while he blessed them, he was separated from them, and ascended into heaven, and sat down at the right hand of God.

[56:13] ,  And they worshipped him, and returned to Jerusalem with great joy: and at all times they were in the temple, praising and blessing God, Amen.

[56:14] And from thence they went forth, and preached in every place; and our Lord helped them, and confirmed their sayings by the signs which they did.

[56:15] And here are also many other things which Jesus did, which if they were written every one of them, not even the world, according to my opinion, would contain the books which should be written.
